Beijing Municipal Government's Budget for the 25th Year: Expense Budget Shortfall of Approximately One Million; Land Tax Levy Reduces Housing Tax 65

Nanjing Communication: The beginning of the 25th year is approaching in an instant. In order to adapt the administrative plan and expense budget for the 25th year to each other, the Beijing Municipal Government is preparing the budget at the same time as drafting the administrative plan. After the plan was sorted out a few days ago, it was sent to the municipal government for review again. According to the person in charge of the municipal government, the details are as follows:

No Increase in Budgeted Standard Revenue

The municipal government's preparation of the budget for the 25th year, in addition to preparing the plan at the same time as adapting to the administrative plan, is also based on the expenses of the 24th year as the standard. According to the city's budget for the 24th year, the regular revenue was 5,657,425 yuan, and the temporary revenue was 3,680,000 yuan, totaling 9,337,425 yuan. Regular expenses were 4,739,919 yuan, and temporary expenses were 4,597,506 yuan, totaling 9,337,425 yuan. The deficit in the budget for the 24th year was originally over 2 million yuan. Because of the difficulty in raising funds, some non-urgent construction projects were postponed, and our expense deficit was reduced to over 1 million yuan. The expense budget for the 25th year is currently being calculated. Generally, it is planned to reduce it to the same amount as the 24th year. At most, the deficit will be between 1.5 million and 2 million yuan.

The municipal government's expenditures are mostly for education, followed by construction expenses such as road construction. In addition to increasing the number of schools and opening up roads, the administrative plan for the 25th year also plans to reorganize the shantytown areas. There are many shantytowns and poor people in the city. If they are not given relief, it will not only hinder the city's appearance, but also pose a problem for the development of their lives. In short, this city is located in the capital area, and there are many construction projects, but because of the difficulty in raising funds, it is difficult to achieve our ideal goals in a short period of time. As for the revenue budget for the 25th year, there is no increase. Although the land tax can be levied starting next year, 30% of the housing tax is stipulated to be deducted, so the land price tax only accounts for 70%. In the future, the total revenue will probably only be about 1 million yuan. Although this budget has been approved, it still needs to be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval.

Housing Tax Collected at 70%

The Beijing Municipal Government originally planned to implement the collection of land tax and improvement tax at the same time starting in the 25th year. At present, the estimation of land prices can be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Land Law. It should not be difficult. The city originally had a Land Valuation Committee, which has a lot of experience in estimating land prices. However, although the estimation of improvements can be done when estimating land prices, it is extremely difficult to estimate old improvements. Even if you ask the owners, they are mostly confused. Moreover, the estimation of improvements actually requires on-site surveys of each household and separate estimations. After the estimation, the owners must be notified, and if there is any objection, a public hearing must be held. Therefore, the estimation of improvements throughout the city cannot be completed in less than two or three years.

Before the improvement tax can be implemented at the same time as the land tax, the municipal government plans to retain the housing tax and reduce it to 70% in order to show consideration for the burden on the citizens. This method has been approved by the Ministry of Interior and can be implemented after the Executive Yuan approves it again. The old housing tax can bring in 600,000 to 700,000 yuan per year. If calculated at 70%, it will be reduced to more than 400,000 yuan. The total amount of land tax is set at 600,000 yuan. The tax rate is currently being submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. According to the current situation, the burden on citizens is actually lighter before the improvement tax is implemented. This is because the municipal government is taking into account both the city's treasury revenue and the burden on citizens. On the one hand, it does not want tax revenue to be short, and on the other hand, it must also take into account the burden on citizens so that there is no feeling of overlapping tax rates.

Taishan Meteorological Observatory Completed: Only High-Altitude Meteorological Observatory in East Asia 66

Beijing News: The Meteorological Research Institute of the Academia Sinica established a meteorological station on the Jade Emperor Peak of Mount Tai in Shandong Province in the 21st year of the Republic of China in order to observe high-altitude meteorological conditions. At that time, the Jade Emperor Hall was temporarily used as a place to store instruments and work. However, old-fashioned houses were very inconvenient for research. Therefore, the construction of a new station began on the top of the mountain in April of last year. Due to weather and altitude, it took one year and two months to complete. A few days ago, Lu Jiong, a full-time researcher at the institute, and Liu Futai, the design engineer of the station, went to inspect and receive it. The walls of the station are all made of granite, about two feet thick, and can withstand the strong winds on the top of the mountain. The total construction cost was more than 30,000 yuan. The station is 5,059 feet above sea level and is the only high-altitude meteorological observatory in East Asia.

A Glimpse of Relief Efforts in Guangdong Province: Dongguan County Builds a Home for the Disabled and Elderly 67

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has spared no effort in promoting relief efforts in recent years, especially in caring for the elderly, weak, and disabled. All counties have been able to pay active attention. Recently, the Dongguan County Relief Home planned to expand its home for the disabled and elderly. It has been learned that since the home successively established facilities for the disabled, the elderly, medical treatment, and loans last year, its internal organization has become more complete. However, the home for the disabled and elderly is limited by space and cannot accommodate many people. As a result, the number of people registering and waiting for admission is increasing daily. Due to the inability to accommodate everyone, the director, Luo Youheng, believes that these poor people are indeed old and helpless, and their situation is particularly pitiful. He applied to the county government to find a way to build additional housing on the vacant land behind the branch home to expand its capacity. Surveying by workers has already been arranged at the home, and everything is being planned. Furthermore, a portion of the home's apprentices are prisoners sent by the county government after their release. Now, considering that many of these released prisoners possess skills and are aware of their past mistakes, the county government, in a gesture of compassion, has ordered the home to select twenty-seven inmates who have been in the home for over a year and have improved their character or are old and weak, and allow them to be released. County Magistrate Deng also visited the home to give a speech, instructing those released to thoroughly reform their past misdeeds and strive to be law-abiding citizens. At the same time, he ordered the home's loan office to lend each person five yuan to help them make a living after their release, with interest-free repayment within six months. He also required them to sign a pledge that they would not engage in any illegal activities after their release, and that if they committed another crime, they would be punished with the most severe penalties. The home also reported that due to the global economic downturn in recent years, there have been several requests each month from unemployed poor people seeking admission. Therefore, to achieve universal relief, it was submitted to the county government for approval to post a notice recruiting thirty apprentices to expand relief efforts.

The Huai River Conservancy Commission: Dredging of the Anfeng Pond Project; 60% of the River Dredging Project Completed 68

Bengbu Correspondence: The Anfeng Pond dredging project in Shouxian County, Anhui Province, is being managed by the Huai River Conservancy Commission with allocated funds. The Anfeng Pond Project Office of the Huai River Conservancy Commission was established in March of this year, and construction began in early April. The first step was to dredge the Biyuan River. The collection of workers was entrusted by the Huai River Conservancy Commission to the Shouxian County Government, which established a labor team management office to be responsible for handling the matter. When workers arrived, each person received an advance of 1.5 yuan for food expenses. Every ten days, the amount of work completed was calculated, with a fixed price of 9.5 cents per cubic foot, including drainage costs. The price was paid according to the amount of work completed. All advance food expenses and work prices were issued by the engineering office to the Shouxian labor team management office for collection and distribution. The Huai River Conservancy Commission and the Shouxian County Government have established detailed construction rules. At the beginning of the project, the work was relatively smooth. However, in early May, due to inadequate management of the labor team, workers scattered and deserted. The Huai River Conservancy Commission, eager to complete the entire project, approved the Shouxian County Government's request to increase the work price by 1.5 cents per cubic foot and advance another 3,000 yuan for food expenses, ordering the county government to continue recruiting workers. It has recently been learned that this is in progress. This dredging project is now 60% complete. It was originally scheduled to be completed by mid-month, but due to this setback, completion is expected by the end of the month or the beginning of next month.

Zhejiang Province Trains Fisheries Instructors; Intended to Improve and Develop Fisheries; Training Conducted by the Aquatic Products Field 69

Zhejiang News: In view of the declining fisheries in the province's coastal areas, the Construction Department has ordered coastal counties to establish fisheries instructors to improve and develop fisheries in the future. It has also ordered Chen Tongbai, director of the Aquatic Products Experiment Field, to establish a fisheries instructor training class at the field, with students selected and sent by various counties for training to ensure practical application. It is reported that the field has been instructed by the provincial government to start classes on September 1. The training regulations, fisheries instructor appointment rules, and service rules have been revised and promulgated by the provincial government. After receiving the order, the field has started preparations, and classrooms and dormitories have been properly arranged. The course schedule is as follows: Academic Subjects: Aquatic Products Administration, Fisheries Cooperatives, Fisheries Enterprises and Organizations, General Fisheries Studies, General Manufacturing Studies, General Aquaculture Studies, Aquatic Products Survey Statistics, Aquatic Products Regulations, General Fisheries Economics, Fisheries Equipment, General Aquatic Zoology and Botany, Overview of Aquatic Products in the Province, General Maritime Knowledge, Extension Materials, and Exercises for Each Subject. Classes will be held for thirty-six hours per week, with senior technical personnel from the field responsible for teaching.

Suzhou: Baoda Money Exchange Closes Down 73

The Baoda Money Exchange on Guanqian Street was established in the summer of 1911 and has a history of twenty-five years. Its usual balance sheet is about two to three million yuan. However, due to the impact of the bankruptcy of Shanghai's Baoda Yutian Sui, it suddenly announced its closure on the previous day (the 23rd), the Dragon Boat Festival. Deposits are about four to five hundred thousand yuan, and only over ten thousand yuan is currently in the store. It has been decided to repay according to a pro-rata basis. The reason for the closure is that the exchange was opened by Shen Xingzhu. Shen also has two and a half shares in Baoda Yu. After Baoda Yu went bankrupt, these two and a half shares were responsible. Shen has been withdrawing, but various creditors are demanding compensation from the Shen family because other shareholders are hiding, causing the independently established Suzhou Baoda to also be brought down. However, the exchange initially wanted to maintain operations. It was not until 10 p.m. on the 23rd that it decided to close.

Wu Yuheng has been transferred to be the presiding judge of the Third Criminal Division. Stolen Coal Dispute Reaches Stalemate 77

The case of the stolen coal in Liujiang has not yet been resolved. The unscrupulous merchants Ma Echu, Zhu Changshou, Lian Yuehun, etc., have all avoided meeting. Yesterday, Feng Bokang and Yang Zhaoqing, representatives of the Zhang Wanyuan warehouse owner, negotiated the cancellation of the lease with the original broker Xin Genji. (Note: After Ma Echu and others organized the Gongda Coal Company, they leased the Zhang Wanyuan Wine Shop as a warehouse, intending to store stolen coal.) At the same time, Feng and Yang questioned Wang Junshi, the representative of Mitsui & Co., on four points: 1. The lessee is Ma Echu, not Mitsui & Co. Mitsui & Co. has no right to directly unload and store stolen coal. 2. The leasing procedures, such as the signing of the contract, the payment of the premium, and the rental balance, have not been completed, so the lease has not been confirmed. Even Ma Echu has no right to use it. 3. The lease date is set for July 5. Before July 5, even Ma Echu cannot arbitrarily unload and store coal, let alone Mitsui & Co., which has no relationship. In particular, Zhu Haoran's prying open the lock and entering is even more illegal and should be dealt with according to law. 4. Dozens of tons of stolen coal have already been unloaded and stored in the warehouse. They should be removed immediately, and those not yet unloaded should not be unloaded. After being questioned, Wang Junshi and others were speechless. The boatmen, due to food problems, mortgaged the anchors on the boats. On the one hand, they also negotiated with the Mitsui representatives. It is heard that Mitsui has ordered the original boats to return to Jiangyin and transport the coal to Shanghai for storage. However, the boatmen are unwilling to load and transport the coal, so negotiations are still ongoing in Wuxi, resulting in a stalemate.

Yangzhou: Cao Juhe Cloth Shop Robbed 78

The home of Xie Binlai, owner of the Cao Juhe Cloth Shop, who moved to Yiju Village in the West Countryside, was suddenly attacked by more than a dozen robbers armed with handguns and wooden sticks around 11 p.m. the night before. The air defense exercise period is set for July 20. This association will send a letter to the Air Defense Committee for review and implementation. 4. It is proposed that the membership fees paid by the members of this association be used to purchase air defense magazines and books for browsing. 5. It is proposed that this association send a letter to the Air Defense Headquarters or branch association to send personnel to Luhe for a week to practice air defense matters to promote publicity.

Hangzhou: Verdict Yesterday on Son Imprisonment Case 81

Zhang Qingxiang, a local tyrant from Liangzhe Town, Hangzhou County, plotted to seize the property of his nephew Mao Song (said to be his own son adopted by his brother), on the pretext that Mao Song was suffering from mental illness, and imprisoned him in a dark room for eight years. After the case was reported, the police were dispatched to rescue Mao Song from danger. The defendant was summoned for interrogation and sent to prison. At 4 p.m. on the 24th, the Hangzhou District Court conducted another interrogation, and the verdict was announced in court. Zhang Qingxiang was sentenced to seven years and six months in prison for continuing to obstruct the freedom of others. If he does not agree, he can file an appeal, otherwise he will be sent to prison to serve his sentence.

Surveying the Eastern Zhejiang Canal 82

The Zhejiang Construction Department, on the order of the National Economic Council, plans to open a canal from Ningbo River through Yuyao, Shaoxing, to the Qiantang River, and plans to dredge a section of the Western Zhejiang Canal to connect the eastern and western water conservancy and navigation in Zhejiang, facilitate irrigation in Ningbo and Shaoxing, and plans to build five gates in Yuyao, Cao'e, Xixing, and other places to open and close the water flow at any time to adjust the water flow to allow the entry and exit of large turntables. A special technician, Yang Jian, will depart on the 25th to survey Xiaoshan, Yuyao, Shaoxing, Ningbo, and other places to facilitate planning and opening up, and transfer to Fenghua Yanxi for surveying, because the county suffers from floods every year and plans to build flood control and water storage reservoirs in the Zhuyuan Village area to prevent floods.

Ningbo: Bandit Convicted in Gaoqiao Kidnapping Case Executed by Firing Squad 83

Huang Qizheng, the bandit involved in the kidnapping and killing of Bao Quanzhong, the manager of the Zhang Xiaoji Winery in Gaoqiao Town, Yinxi, was captured by the Fenghua Self-Defense Corps. The Yinqu District Security Command sent a team to the headquarters for interrogation. According to his confession, he was guilty of conspiracy to rob, shoot, kill, and kidnap, and was sentenced to death. The sentence was submitted to the Provincial Security Command for approval, and the bandit was executed by firing squad on the spot. At 10 a.m. yesterday, a platoon of soldiers escorted the bandit to the scene of the incident in Gaoqiao to carry out the execution by firing squad.

Taizhou: Issuance of Strict Prohibition Against Water Cutting 84

Recently, unscrupulous merchants have been found in Wenling City to collect and exchange hard currency, cutting twelve boards of copper coins for water and buying one yuan of silver coins from the people. The general ignorant residents, seeing the profit to be made, have successively sold them. Now the county government has issued a strict prohibition. It is heard that those who collect and exchange coins have gradually disappeared.

Educational Broadcast Special Publication

Lecture on Biology 2: How to Study Biology in the Future 85

— Xue Deyu

Among all the fields of learning, biology has the deepest relationship with human life, but the general youth in our country often regard it as unimportant. What kind of learning is biology? Why should we study biology? Last time, I talked about the contributions of biology to mankind. Today, I want to talk about "How to Study Biology in the Future."

Why should we study biology? We can talk about why we should study biology from both theoretical and practical aspects. From a theoretical point of view: human beings and other organisms follow the same evolutionary path, so why is the position occupied by human beings in nature significantly different from other organisms? From an organizational point of view, human beings are far inferior to lions and tigers. They have neither defensive organs nor strong physical strength. Why can they be the spirit of all things? I think this is a gift from human beings' management of social life. We must first recognize clearly that "it is not human beings who create society, but society that creates human beings." If you don't believe it, you can present evidence. Try taking a child from the Miao ethnic group, put him in our social education, and after he becomes an adult, he can do the same career as us and make the same contribution; if you send a child of a civilized person to be raised in the Miao ethnic group, even if he is intelligent, he will be useless and make no contribution in his life; therefore, whether a person makes a contribution to the world depends on whether there is a society behind him. Although human beings and bees also have societies, their societies have reached their extreme and cannot be improved further; while human societies are flourishing and progressing and developing forward.

The origin of human society is the family. The system of one husband and one wife not only originates from the impulse of sexual desire but also from the care and education of descendants. The reproductive period of human infants is longer than that of all other organisms. Therefore, couples have various relationships and have to have a permanent family organization. Since there is a family, there is a parent. The people of a family need to be controlled and ruled by the parent. In other words, the people of a family must obey the parent with a central force and have no absolute freedom.

In biological principles, weak animals can also resist strong enemies by uniting together. Ants and bedbugs are examples. For the sake of self-defense and to cooperate in resisting enemies, human beings form tribes from families and villages from tribes. With a strong central force and a spirit of obedience, there is progress in human society today. Because society is organized by individuals, the two spirits of "individualism" and "centralized power" are bound to compete with each other. The history of the struggle between these two spirits forms the history of mankind. We use the eyes of biology to investigate the experience of human progress, so that the origin of all ideological problems and social problems can be thoroughly understood and reasonably resolved. If we do not think from the source and want to engage in improving society, it is like climbing a tree to catch a fish, which is impossible. As for improving races, revitalizing nations, and improving domestic animals and crops, without basing on the theory of genetics, there will be no satisfactory results. Moreover, human health care and various industrial problems should be based on biology, so biologists should stand on the front line of society as general commanders, so that human civilization can become more prosperous.

From a practical point of view: hemp, cotton, wool, silk, and other clothing materials, dyes for dyeing clothes, grains, vegetables, fruits, meat, eggs, and other food materials, tea and coffee and other beverages, wood and other building materials or fuels, pathogens that cause diseases, and various medicinal materials for treating diseases. In short, the materials for clothing, food, and housing, and the raw materials for manufacturing industries, are all used by organisms and have a close relationship with human life.

How is biology divided into subjects? From theoretical and practical aspects, we have our own need to study biology. Biology began with past zoology and botany. The purpose of the two is the same, but the methods are different. The latter—zoology and botany—emphasizes records (recording objects), classification (identifying objects), and uses (using objects); the former—biology—emphasizes experience, reasoning, and attention to natural phenomena and principles of life. With the progress of the times, biology has been divided into many subjects. Based on the nature of each subject, it can be divided into the following three categories:

(A) Pure Biology Pure biology belongs to the science of theory, so it is also called Theoretical Biology. Depending on the type of object, it can be divided into three groups for convenience: "Zoology," "Botany," and "Anthropology." Each group can be further divided into "Morphology" and "Physiology." Morphology is also called the Science of Construction. It specializes in the morphology and structure of organisms and seeks their system from the comparison of mutual structures between races. It is further divided into "Organology," "Anatomy" (Histology, Cytology, Nuclear Science), "Embryology," and "Taxonomy." Physiology is the Science of Vital Phenomena. In a broad sense, it can also be considered the Science of Life. It is based on "Physiology," which discusses various principles of life, and includes "Ecology," which discusses the relationship between life activities and the external environment, and "Genetics," which discusses the generational relationship between systematic individuals.

(B) Human Biology Human biology is to discuss what impact various life phenomena carried out in animal and plant bodies have on the life activities of the human body? What kind of impact does the existence of a certain organism and its life activities have on human life? What is the relationship between the action of organisms on the inorganic world and human life? In summary, human biology is to discuss the ecological relationship between human life and biological life based on matters related to human life.

(C) Applied Biology How to use organisms that can be used as materials for clothing, food, housing, and raw materials for manufacturing industries? How to expand knowledge related to human life? This is the scope of research of applied biology. The types and various products we need in our daily life are all bestowed by applied biology. In terms of making a profit, there are subjects such as agronomy, forestry, manufacturing industry, agricultural manufacturing, horticulture, sericulture, animal husbandry, aquatic product manufacturing, and aquatic product fishing. The scope of application is expanding year by year, and the number of subjects is also increasing year by year. Therefore, the relationship between biology and human life is becoming closer, and its progress is not only directly related to the life of individuals but can also increase the country's wealth.

Our Research Goals Biology has pure biology and applied biology. Should we focus on pure biology, or applied biology? From a historical perspective, concrete sciences are all developed from practical knowledge, and practical use precedes and progresses more than theory. For example, botany originated from materia medica, useful plants, and horticulture; yeast in fermentation; hygiene in diseases; breeding experiments in edible plants and hybridization, etc. Therefore, some people advocate that learning without practical benefits has no value in research. This extreme view of focusing on applied biology and neglecting pure biology is also wrong. For example, the research of Leavenhoek and Pasteur, two pure biologists, mentioned last time. When they were doing research, they did not dream that this research would contribute greatly to the world. Their purpose was only to explore the truth and expand human intelligence. As a result, we were able to fight against pathogens in health and gain many benefits in food storage. These are all thanks to pure scientists. Therefore, we must not regard pure biology as useless learning, at least to understand that scholars who seek the truth can often produce great undertakings that affect the world and human beings. If we sit in a well and look at the sky, and only focus on practical benefits, we will hinder the progress of human intelligence.

Various Groups Held a Meeting Yesterday and Decided to Organize an Anti-Smuggling Association 86

Published Declaration Announces All Sectors Uniting to Assist the Government in Reporting Smuggled Goods, Punishing Traitors, and Electing Wang Xiaolai and 35 Others as Committee Members

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation convened a joint meeting of representatives from its affiliated trade associations and various groups at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday at 2 PM to discuss ways to address the smuggling problem. Attendees included Cao Zhigong, Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, Chen Jiufeng, Wang Jingdong from the City Federation; Jiang Wanping from the Shanghai Institute of Certified Public Accountants; Gu Chengan from the Bankers' Association; Zhou Linxiang from the Watch Industry Association; Chen Chunrong from the Sand Boat Industry Association; Sun Choucheng from the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association; Yu Yaoqiu from the Southern Goods Industry Association; Wang Hanqiang from the National Products Preservation Association; Liu Zhongying from the China National Products Manufacturers United Association; Lu Xingzhuang from the National Products Factories United Association; Jin Chuxiang from the Salted Fish Industry Association; and over a hundred others.

Chairman's Report

After formalities were observed, Chairman Cao Zhigong delivered a report, stating in brief: "Recently, smuggling has become rampant in North China. Smuggling significantly impacts national treasury revenue and severely harms the entire national economy. They use a dumping policy to bring smuggled goods into the country, and people often buy them because of their low prices, obstructing the sales of domestic products. Therefore, all sectors of the city should, on the one hand, awaken the people to resist purchasing smuggled goods and, on the other hand, assist the government in investigating and cracking down on smuggling. Resolutions

Regarding the case of "How to nominate candidates for the establishment of an investigation committee," it was resolved that the investigation committee members would be respectively responsible by various trade associations, labor unions, and district branches of the City Federation, with the list to be announced after confirmation. Regarding the case of "Nominating the drafting of the organization outline and work outline," it was resolved to nominate Cao Zhigong, Gu Yucang, and Zhu Yutao to draft. Regarding the case of "Publishing a declaration of establishment," it was resolved to pass it. Regarding the case of "How to express concern about Japan's increasing troops in North China, which damages our national sovereignty," it was resolved to telegraph the central government to conduct serious negotiations and immediately announce the abolition of the outdated Boxer Protocol. Regarding the case of "Telegraphing the authorities of Guangdong and Guangxi, calling for peace and unity against external aggression," it was resolved to telegraph the Guangdong and Guangxi authorities to withdraw the advancing troops.

Publication of Declaration

The declaration states: "The means by which imperialists invade other countries is through military threats with the goal of economic exploitation. For the past century, our country has been under the political and economic oppression of imperialism. Our territory has shrunk day by day, our sovereignty has been eroded, and our national economy is on the verge of exhaustion. In recent times, the development of capitalism has become increasingly contradictory. Therefore, their exploitation of small countries or colonies is becoming increasingly brutal. The September 18th Incident proves the urgency of this situation. Now, the provinces in North China are under the control of a certain force and are in imminent danger. The vagrant Japanese and traitors, protected by special powers, are engaged in rampant tax evasion and smuggling. Customs duties are thus undermined, credit is affected, and national industrial and commercial enterprises are assaulted, plunging them into a situation from which they cannot recover. This city is a major port in East Asia and the economic center of the country. Water and land transportation are extremely convenient. It is also a gathering place for merchants of all kinds, both good and bad. If the vagrant Japanese and traitors use this as their base for tax evasion and smuggling, the consequences will be unimaginable. All sectors of this city are pained by the brutality of imperialist economic aggression and the impending doom of national subjugation. Therefore, the Shanghai All-Circles Anti-Smuggling Association has been established, hoping to assist the government in reporting smuggled goods and punishing traitors from the standpoint of popular autonomy in order to maintain the economic lifeline of the country. We hope that all compatriots across the country will unite to eliminate smuggled goods. The future of the nation relies on this. This declaration is hereby made."

Chamber of Commerce Requests Ministry of Industry to Implement Industrial Control 87

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce again submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry yesterday, urging the implementation of industrial control, stating: "Regarding the matter of the Chamber submitting a request, the Chamber investigated that in April of last year, in order to save the decline of industry, it was appropriate to start with controlling production to avoid excess. It drafted sixteen articles of the Regulations for Industrial Control and submitted them to your ministry for adoption and implementation. Because it had not been approved for a long time, it submitted a document urging it. On September 6 of that year, the Ministry issued Directive No. 13241 of the Department of Industry, stating that this matter had been communicated to the provincial and municipal governments for discussion and reply, and that it would be obeyed after the collection and review of the specific plan, etc. At the same time, it also checked the Ministry's reply to the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, stating that the provinces and cities that had responded to the Ministry included Guangxi, Jiangxi, Sichuan, Ningxia, Chahar, Shaanxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Guizhou, as well as Nanjing, Shanghai, and Peiping. In January of the 25th year, the Chamber again submitted a request for investigation and on the 21st of that month, it received Directive No. 14432 of the Department of Industry, stating that this matter was of great importance to the entire industrial future of the country, and that it should still wait for the provincial and municipal governments to review the previous case and reply to the Ministry before proceeding with the review. This matter has been submitted by the Chamber for more than a year. Whether there have been any further opinions received in addition to the nine provinces and three cities mentioned above, although it is impossible to speculate, the adjustment of national industries is related to the current tightening of foreign goods invasion, and the national industry is in danger of immediate collapse. Survival is at stake. It seems that it should not be delayed due to the delay of the provincial documents. In recent years, such as the silkworm silk control in Zhejiang Province, the silkworm seed control in Jiangsu Province, the black tea transport and sales control in Anhui and Jiangxi, and the industrial and commercial control in Shanxi and Guangdong provinces, the scope is even wider. According to reports, Guangxi Province also intends to control the main products to be exported from the province first. If the central government does not have a unified plan and regulations to improve its aftermath, it will inevitably make a country become countless economic groups, which will only increase chaos and hinder the sales of domestic merchants. In view of the domestic and international situation, the promulgation of the Industrial Control Regulations is really difficult to delay any longer. Therefore, the Seventh Members' Congress resolved to submit another request to your ministry to formulate the regulations as soon as possible so that they can be implemented as soon as possible. It is in the file for your information. It is respectfully requested that the Ministry review and approve the implementation, which will be convenient for the public."

Commodity Inspection Bureau Investigates Pests in Stored Grain, Resulting in Considerable Annual Losses 90

"The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, with Shanghai as the industrial and commercial center, the warehousing industry, the rice mill industry, and the flour mill industry, developed as the national champion. The general occurrence of grain pests causes considerable annual losses. Experts were specially assigned to investigate, and the results are now available. The reporter from the East China News Agency briefly records the situation as follows:

Pest Situation in Warehouses

Warehouses that are ravaged by grain pests are mostly not ventilated, not exposed to sunlight, are in humid locations, and have many gaps, giving pests the opportunity to breed. Climate factors such as temperature and humidity can directly affect the breeding of pests. If the temperature and humidity of a certain period are suitable for the reproduction and development of a certain pest in the warehouse, the pest will be rampant. The grain pests found in warehouses often appear in garbage, debris, and crevices. Grain pests are mostly omnivorous and can chew on a variety of grains for food. If grain is constantly available, pests can survive for a long time. Shanghai is a gathering place for boats and vehicles, and goods are moved in and out all year round, so pests have many opportunities to spread.

Complex Types of Stored Grain Pests

The stored grain pests that occur in warehouses are very complex, and the quantity is (A) Moths: One-spot grain moth, Large-spot moth, Indian grain moth, Wheat moth; (B) Beetles: Grain weevil, Mung bean weevil, Red flour beetle, Large flour beetle, Black cocoon beetle, are all very harmful."

Rice Mill Pests Estimate Five Types

The most harmful is the one-spot grain moth, which spreads along both banks of the Suzhou River. The large flour beetle spreads in Xinzha Road and the aforementioned areas. The black sesame beetle and the red flour beetle spread in the rice mills on Gongguan Road and Tiantong Road. The large beetle thief is also found in excellent white rice, but it has the habit of preying on other pests and cannibalizing itself, so it can also be called a beneficial insect.

Few Found in Flour Mills

All kinds of flour mills in Shanghai are well managed. The stacking of flour bags is very orderly. The location and construction of the warehouses are often in line with high, ventilated, light, and clean conditions, so there are fewer pests. However, in the wheat warehouse, with gray walls and broken grains all over the floor, grain weevils are very rampant, eroding the wheat, making the wheat grains empty and turning them into grain crumbs. In addition, there are also wheat moths, large flour beetles, grain thieves, etc., which are also quite a few types.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Cocoon Shops Have Stopped Weighing; The Syndicate Has Stopped Lending 94

A total of 11.5 million yuan has been lent; the matter of the borrowers returning the money is already being handled

The New Sound News Agency learned from the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Spring Cocoon Purchase and Loan Syndicate in the 25th year that after handling the silk manufacturers and surplus cocoon merchants to purchase cocoons and lend money, the syndicate has lent a total of 30 million yuan. The initial deadline was May 20 in Zhejiang and May 25 in Jiangsu, and then a special extension was granted. They could also apply for additional loans at any time as needed for cocoon purchase. Now the local cocoon shops in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have stopped weighing one after another. The Shanghai General Office and the Hangzhou and Wuxi branch offices have all suspended cocoon purchase and lending and are only handling the silk manufacturers and surplus cocoon merchants who have borrowed money to return the money. This time, a total of 11.5 million yuan has been lent, with Jiangsu accounting for 70-80% and Zhejiang accounting for 10-20%, which is distributed according to the proportion of the number of loans borne by the banks and Qian Zhuang shops participating in the syndicate. A meeting of the committee's banks and Qian Zhuang shops will be held regularly to report on the details of the loans and handle the end. It is heard that the syndicate's cocoon purchase and lending has benefited farmers and merchants a lot. Therefore, when the autumn cocoons are on the market this year, it is planned to reorganize the "Jiangsu and Zhejiang Autumn Cocoon Purchase and Loan Syndicate in the 25th Year" to handle the autumn cocoon lending. The specific measures are still under discussion."

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Submits to the Ministry of Finance: Requesting Relief for Domestic Tobacco Leaf 98

Ningbo Native Association Sends Letters to the Ministries of Finance and Industry

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "This is a petition to request relief based on the circumstances. During the seventh session of the Member Representative Assembly held by the association on June 20th, a letter was received from the local tobacco leaf industry association, stating that a certain local newspaper had reported that the government intended to implement unified control of tobacco leaves, and it was rumored that this so-called unified control was actually a euphemism for monopoly. Although detailed measures have not yet been promulgated, the matter is inevitable. If this matter is implemented, the entire tobacco leaf industry will inevitably become unemployed, and those who sell tobacco leaves, directly and indirectly, number no less than hundreds of thousands. Once there is no business to operate, how will they make a living? The association is deeply concerned about the difficulties of the times and offers the following suggestions and six measures, regarding improving tobacco leaves, promoting domestic products, preventing raw materials for private cigarettes to enrich national taxes, and improving the industry. These are merely humble opinions, and the implementation measures still need to be discussed and determined in the future. However, once the outline is in place, the details will be easy to discuss. If the government's unified control of tobacco leaves is solely for the purpose of preventing tobacco leaves from supplying raw materials for private cigarettes and there is no intention to fundamentally eliminate the tobacco leaf industry, then the above-mentioned measures of the association will not only be for the survival of the industry but also for the government's benefit." The association also attached its opinions and measures regarding the production of domestic tobacco leaves, which were submitted to the assembly for resolution and referred to the executive committee for deliberation. It has been found that in recent years, due to the encroachment of foreign goods and the desire for high quality, most domestic cigarette manufacturers have adopted foreign tobacco. The American tobacco grown in Henan, Shandong, and other places is mostly purchased by foreign tobacco factories. Privately produced cigarettes are rampant in the interior, which not only deals a major blow to domestic cigarettes but also has a significant impact on tax revenue. The opinions and measures provided are indeed for the sake of rescuing the entire domestic tobacco and tobacco tax industry. Therefore, the association has compiled the opinions and measures attached by the industry and presented them for consideration and adoption by the ministry for the public convenience."

Letter from the Ningbo Native Association

The Shen Shi News Agency reports that the Ningbo Native Association in Shanghai, based on a letter from the tobacco leaf industry association stating that the government intends to monopolize tobacco leaves, sent separate letters to the Ministries of Finance and Industry yesterday, requesting that the matter be dropped to alleviate the difficulties of businesses. The original letter stated: "We respectfully submit the following. According to a letter from the Shanghai Tobacco Leaf Industry Association, we have learned that the production of tobacco in our country has a long history. Provinces such as Hunan, Henan, Fujian, Guangdong, Hubei, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui all have large-scale production. Although the varieties differ, they are all used for the manual production of water and dry tobacco, which is what is now called local tobacco. Since the influence of European trends in the East, foreigners have established cigarette factories in our country and worked hard to dump their products. Within a few years, they became popular throughout the country. At that time, the raw materials for the cigarettes produced by foreign factories were all transported from foreign countries (i.e., American tobacco). As a result, tobacco-producing areas throughout our country were greatly affected, and tobacco farmers suffered unspeakable hardships. Later, far-sighted people in our country, feeling that money was flowing out, also started to establish cigarette manufacturing factories, intending to use domestic tobacco leaves as the standard. However, domestic tobacco leaves are all sun-dried, resulting in a special odor when rolled into paper cigarettes, which is not suitable for cigarette use. Therefore, most Chinese factories also switched to using imported American tobacco, resulting in a year-by-year increase in foreign tobacco imports. Subsequently, foreign factories, relying on their strong capital, colluded with unscrupulous merchants to introduce American tobacco seeds into inland Shandong (Qingzhou) and Henan (Xuzhou) to grow cured tobacco. The annual output is about 9,000 tons each. The harvested tobacco leaves all belong to foreign factories, which purchase them at the lowest prices. In particular, Chinese people are not allowed to intervene in Xuzhou, Henan. Although our Chinese factories can obtain some tobacco supply, foreign factories have this cheap and high-quality raw material, and their dumping is even more intense and their profits are greater. Chinese factories cannot compete with them, and our tobacco leaf industry deeply feels that domestic tobacco leaves are declining. In order to prevent money from flowing out and to alleviate the suffering of tobacco farmers, they jointly organized a Domestic Tobacco Leaf Improvement Committee, reviewed domestic geology, raised funds to purchase American tobacco seeds from overseas, and sent personnel to Xuzhou in Henan and the seven nearby counties, as well as Qingzhou in Shandong, to distribute the seeds to farmers to plant American tobacco. They were cured by artificial coal-fired heating. As a result, the color and taste of Xuzhou (produced in seven counties) were the best, and they were suitable for cigarette use. Qingzhou was second. The tobacco leaves were evaluated and purchased by the industry to supply the needs of Chinese factories. Since then, the products of Chinese factories have been excellent and sales have increased sharply. Factories have adopted the methods one after another. Not only has the business of foreign factories gradually been hit, but the amount of imported tobacco leaves has also decreased year by year. Recently, domestic cured tobacco has sold well. The annual output of Xuzhou cured tobacco alone reaches 30,000 tons, and Qingzhou has also been increasing year by year. National tax revenues have increased and people's livelihoods have improved. Soon, the loopholes will be closed. Tobacco farmers can sell their tobacco leaves and do not have to sell to foreign factories at suppressed prices. The industry is privately pleased. However, they do not rest on their laurels and stop there. They still strive to catch up, striving to further improve tobacco leaves, improve business, and prevent the supply of raw materials for private cigarettes, in order to promote domestic products and stop the smuggling. However, a certain local newspaper recently reported that the government intends to implement unified control of tobacco leaves, and it was rumored that this so-called unified control was actually a euphemism for monopoly. Although detailed measures have not yet been promulgated, the matter is inevitable. If this matter is implemented, the entire tobacco leaf industry will inevitably become unemployed, and those who sell tobacco leaves, directly and indirectly, number no less than hundreds of thousands. If they lose their jobs, how will they make a living? The association is deeply concerned about the difficulties of the times and offers the following suggestions and five measures, regarding improving tobacco leaves, promoting domestic products, preventing raw materials for private cigarettes to enrich national taxes, and improving the industry. These are merely humble opinions, and the implementation measures still need to be discussed and determined in the future. If the government's unified control of tobacco leaves is solely for the purpose of preventing tobacco leaves from supplying raw materials for private cigarettes and there is no intention to fundamentally eliminate the tobacco leaf industry, then the above-mentioned measures of the association will not only be for the survival of the industry but also for the government's benefit. We hope that the government, which cares for businesses and people, will approve it. Your association has the same native ties and shares the same fate. We sincerely request that you forward the measures proposed by our association to the Ministries of Finance and Industry for adoption." The association has found that the industry's proposed measures are quite thorough in their intentions. In view of the aforementioned situation, the association has copied and attached the five measures and sent a letter to request verification and approval. We would be deeply grateful if you would grant adoption. Respectfully requesting a reply. Respectfully submitted to Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance and Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industry.

Proposed Measures

The Shanghai Tobacco Leaf Industry Association has proposed five measures, which are to be forwarded by the Ningbo Native Association to the Ministries of Finance and Industry for adoption and implementation. The measures are listed below: A tobacco leaf general market should be established in Xuchang, Henan, and several tobacco leaf branch markets should be established in various counties, towns, and villages to facilitate the purchase of tobacco leaves by the industry. A cured tobacco factory should be established in Xuchang, Henan. Because the tobacco leaves in Xuchang are cured by tobacco farmers using traditional methods, the crude manufacturing is not perfect, and there are often poisonous, rotten, and discolored leaves. It is necessary to establish a cured tobacco factory on the spot for the industry to re-cure. Once the goods are completed, the tax authority will send personnel to the factory to add a tax-paid stamp before they can be transported to Shanghai for storage. A responsible transportation office should be established in Xuchang, Henan, and Hankou to transport the tobacco leaves purchased by various industries in Shanghai. Only tobacco leaves that have undergone the curing process can be shipped. A tobacco leaf public warehouse should be established in Shanghai, or two warehouses, specifically for storing cured tobacco for the industry. The Ministry of Finance and the Tax Authority should be requested to send personnel to the factory to monitor and prevent the supply of raw materials for private cigarettes. A joint business office for the tobacco industry should be established in Shanghai to handle all business operations of the industry. The most perfect method of organization should be discussed by the industry in conjunction with the tax authority. After its establishment, the joint business office will be the general organ. The markets for purchasing tobacco leaves in the producing areas, as well as the Xuchang cured tobacco factory and the transportation offices in Xuchang and Hankou, will all be affiliated with the joint business office. With a dedicated authority, and with frequent correspondence via letters and telegrams, the situation can be reviewed at any time.

Ding Xie-lin Discusses Changes in the Ionosphere During Solar Eclipse Observation 99

The Results Are Very Satisfactory

Mr. Ding Xielin, Director of the Institute of Physics of the National Central Research Institute, gave a speech yesterday, saying that the structure of the ionosphere is an important issue in geophysics. The impact of solar eclipses on the ionosphere is of great research value. Therefore, during each solar eclipse, scholars from various countries, in addition to observing changes in astronomy and meteorology, also study changes in the ionosphere. On the 19th of this month, there happened to be a solar eclipse. The institute began preparations several months ago. During the solar eclipse, the critical frequency method of radio waves was used to observe the impact of the solar eclipse on the ionization intensity of the ionosphere, and the reflection method was used to determine the change in its apparent height. In order to reduce the interference of external objects on the instrument during observation, the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation was requested to order the broadcasting stations in the city to stop broadcasting from 1:00 p.m. to 3:00 p.m. on the 18th and 19th of this month. Fortunately, all broadcasting stations were enthusiastic about scientific research and stopped broadcasting as requested. The official observations of the institute were conducted from the 17th to the 21st of this month. The results were extremely satisfactory. It was verified that the F layer and E layer of the ionosphere had significant changes during the solar eclipse. At the beginning of the eclipse, the critical frequency of the two layers was lower than usual. At the maximum eclipse, the critical frequency was even lower. Then, it gradually returned. After the eclipse ended, the critical frequency also returned to normal. Another impact was that the height of the FZ layer was also greater during the solar eclipse than usual. It is worth noting that this solar eclipse was a partial eclipse in Shanghai, but it already had a significant impact. The impact during a total eclipse should be even greater. Therefore, the total solar eclipse in the Yangtze River area in 1941 is a good opportunity to conduct this observation. The institute is planning to conduct more complete research at that time. The person in charge of this research is Mr. Chen Maokang, a researcher at the institute. The assistants in this study were assistant researcher Zhu Enlong and graduate student Liang Baixian. The detailed results are being sorted and drafted and will be published in a professional journal. The success of this study is due to the support of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau and the sacrifice of the broadcasting stations in the city in stopping broadcasting. The institute is very grateful.

Political and Business Leaders Provide Support, All Tea Industry Groups Participate

At the beginning of this year, domestic tea industry academics and tea merchant leaders, at the call of the National Economic Commission, met in the capital to discuss the technical improvement of the tea industry. Recently, Mr. Wang Zhenhuan, chairman of the association (manager of the local Wang Yifa Tea Company), believed that without local tea industry groups as the backbone and without close contact with political and business leaders, it would be difficult to plan for the development of practical affairs. Cousin Abducts Cousin 104

Yu Jitang Has Been Detained in the French Concession, Transferred to the Public Security Bureau Due to the Case Occurring in the Chinese Territory

Wang Ziwen, a local resident, 46 years old, has been running a Maoshun grocery store at No. 26 North Street, Xujiahui Town, West Shanghai, also selling rice straw. He is doing well in business. His wife, Mrs. Huang, gave birth to four daughters. The youngest daughter, Xingxing, is only two years old and is currently being nursed by Zhang Chen, a Jiangyin native, at No. 2 Tong'an Lane, Qian Hu's residence. Wang has a nephew, Yu Jitang, 22 years old, who is known for his low character and idleness. Since he lost his mother at a young age, Wang raised him. He usually works in the store. A month ago, Yu Jitang sold the straw privately and spent the money. He also disappeared. Unexpectedly, the other day (the 23rd), Jitang suddenly came to Tong'an Lane and took his cousin Xingxing away. He did not return that evening. Knowing that something was wrong, they reported it to Wang Ziwen and his wife and then to the police station in charge, requesting an investigation. They also asked people to search everywhere, but there was no sign of her. Until about 1:00 p.m. yesterday, Wang was passing by Xixinqiao, Fada Road, when he saw Yu Jitang whispering with two strangers on the side of the street. Wang grabbed him. The other two escaped. Later, when the patrolman arrived, they took him back to the Songshan Road police station for questioning. Yu confessed that Xingxing was now in the home of Mrs. Zhao Li, a Changzhou woman, on the upper floor of No. 567 Fada Road. The patrol chief sent detectives to bring back Mrs. Zhao Li and witness Xiao Wang, together with Xingxing, to the police station. Because the case occurred in the Chinese territory, the Xuhui police station was notified, and Detective Hu Zongxi brought the offenders back. Yesterday, the chief questioned them separately. According to the plaintiff Wang Ziwen's description of the encounter, the defendant Yu Jitang bowed his head without a word. Mrs. Zhao Li confessed that the girl was brought by Yu and said that her parents had died and there was no one to support her. She paid 3 yuan for the travel expenses. Witness Xiao Wang's confession was the same as Mrs. Zhao Li's. After hearing the confessions, the chief believed that the case involved a cousin abducting his cousin, which was illegal. Therefore, he prepared a document and sent it to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for strict punishment according to the law.

Dyeing Industry Union Strives to Waive Stamp Duty for Workers' Monthly Fees 108

The City Party Department is Requested to Consult the Court Not to Accept the Case, and to Submit a Request to the Central Government for Interpretation of the Trade Union Law

Da Gong News Agency reports that the Shanghai Dyeing and Weaving Industry Union's receipts for monthly fees paid to workers were deemed by stamp tax inspectors to have failed to affix stamp duty. The union filed a lawsuit in the Shanghai Local Court. This matter affects the affairs of workers' groups. Based on Article 34 of the Trade Union Law, which stipulates that trade unions are exempt from income tax, business tax, and registration tax, a request was submitted to the City Party Department to consult the court not to accept the case, and to submit a request to the central government for interpretation, in order to uphold the law. The original presentation is as follows: "We hereby present that the receipts of trade unions which should not be affixed with stamp tax, please consult the court not to accept the case, and please submit the request to the Central Government for interpretation, so as not to affect the entire labor industry. It is found that Article 34 of the fourth section of the protection clauses of the Trade Union Law stipulates, 'Trade unions are exempt from income tax, business tax, and registration tax.' The monthly fees collected by trade unions from workers and the receipts issued are not comparable to business bills and receipts. The exemption provisions have been clearly stipulated in the legal articles. Now, the stamp tax enforcement inspection agency of Shanghai City is ignorant of the law and recklessly regards the monthly fee receipts issued by the union to the workers of Ruihe Dyeing Factory on Lumeng Road, South City, as failing to affix stamp duty, violating the criminal law. The receipts were used as evidence and a lawsuit was filed in the Shanghai Local Court. The court did not refer to the labor laws and regulations, and did not criticize them, but accepted the examination. After the first summons, in addition to responding to the court in accordance with the law, the union submitted a request to the General Labor Union to consult the court and notify the trade unions of various industries, so as to avoid being subject to the same case. Unexpectedly, the court still summoned the union on June 24 and scheduled a hearing for June 30. The provisions of the Trade Union Law are very clear and do not allow for argument. However, the stamp tax inspectors have no common sense of the law. This matter concerns the future of the entire Chinese labor movement. The union has now taken the brunt of it. In order to respect the central laws and regulations and to protect the labor movement, we cannot remain silent. Therefore, we specially present this request to your department to consult the Shanghai Local Court to dismiss this case, and to criticize the stamp tax inspection agency. Now that this matter has already occurred, the latter will follow one after another, which is inevitable. In order for the national labor organizations to implement the law, please submit the request to the Central Government for detailed interpretation and public announcement in the newspapers, so that all sectors of society can understand. This is our sincere prayer."

The Standard Milk Company at No. 60 Nanxun Road, with a capital of 200,000 yuan, began selling and modifying milk in June of the year before last. The business was quite good for a time. Later, due to differences between Chinese and foreign shareholders, excessive spending by foreigners, and poor turnover, the British court ruled in May of this year that all business and assets should be sold. All debts will be cleared by the seller and will not be related to the buyer. According to a report at a meeting of creditors at 3:00 p.m. yesterday, a Westerner submitted a bid to purchase the company and continue operations for 30,000 yuan. However, the price was too low. The machinery alone is worth 60,000 yuan. Even with depreciation by half, it is still worth 30,000 yuan. Therefore, creditor Lu Meiseng proposed and passed on the spot that the deadline be extended by two days to seek a Chinese buyer. Gao Jianfu's Teacher-Student Art Exhibition - Day One 111

The Chinese painting exhibition of Mr. Gao Jianfu and his students, organized by Cai Yuanpei, Sun Ke, Wu Tiecheng, and others, opened yesterday at 10:00 AM. Over five hundred Chinese and foreign visitors attended. Mr. Fasz Ses from Hungary and Mr. Zou Ludan, the director of the Asia Museum, came specifically from Beijing to Shanghai to view the exhibition, praising Gao's work particularly. Gao has loved painting since childhood, diligently copying ancient books, capturing their essence. Later, he studied Western painting in Japan, incorporating its features, and also drawing from the styles of India and Persia, integrating them to create a new eclectic Chinese painting style. This exhibition features sixty-six of Gao's finest works, including his representative works from the first period, "Autumn Wind," the second period, "Mad Prayer," and the third period, "Green Willows in Misty Haze," all crafted with exquisite skill, with rich colors and a particularly bold and elegant brushstroke. There are also one hundred works by his accomplished students, including Fang Rending, Rong Dakui, Dong Aihong, and Wu Gonghu, all of whom have captured Gao's spirit. In addition, there are seventy ancient paintings from the Ming and Qing dynasties collected by Gao. The exhibition is being held at the 2nd floor of the International General Assembly Hall, No. 722 Jing'an Temple Road. The exhibition will run until the 28th, with viewing hours from 10:00 AM to 7:00 PM daily. Admission tickets are sold at the entrance for fifty cents each.

Recent News of the Chinese Cultural Relics Exhibition 112

The Chinese Cultural Relics Exhibition, located at the corner of Jing'an Temple Road and Xining Road, is a joint effort of dozens of Chinese and foreign collectors. Among the exhibits are three thousand items, most of which are rarely seen masterpieces of art from past dynasties. These include ink stones produced by the Lu Xiang Yuan garden, covering nine mu of land in the Ming Dynasty, ancient porcelain from the Song Dynasty, a porcelain coffin of Empress Dowager of Song Huizong, Tantric Buddhist statues made in Tibet during the Ming and Qing Dynasties, and calligraphy and paintings by Ming Dynasty masters Wen Zhengming and Tang Bohu. Many pieces came from the items to be displayed at the Palace Museum of British exhibitions. It is now reported that the exhibition will be adding new steel ware and famous porcelain objects, etc. Without space to display all items, it has been decided to replace the current exhibits soon. The exhibition hours are from 12:30 PM to 8:00 PM daily, and on Sundays from 10:00 AM to 8:00 PM.

Lawyer Yue's Reply

Please inform CPA Wang for review and processing. Therefore, we are responding with this letter for your reference. Sincerely, Yue Junwei, Lawyer.
